<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png/revision/latest?cb=20230904000034" class="image"><img alt="Lucci and Hattori at Enies Lobby" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lucci and Hattori at Enies Lobby.png" data-image-key="Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230904000034"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png/revision/latest?cb=20230904000034" class="image"><img alt="Lucci and Hattori at Enies Lobby" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230904000034" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lucci and Hattori at Enies Lobby.png" data-image-key="Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b7/Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230904000034"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lucci_and_Hattori_at_Enies_Lobby.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci's usual cold look.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci comes off as a cold, distant, and collected <a href="/wiki/Cipher_Pol" title="Cipher Pol">Cipher Pol</a> agent; almost completely psychopathic and amoral of everything around him. A testament to his cold-blooded nature is his brutal assault on his "friend" of five years, Paulie, whom he even tried to kill after the CP9's identities were revealed.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">[20]</a></sup> He also stated that he felt no true bond with the city of <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a> which he lived in for five years,<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup> and had no concern for his superior <a href="/wiki/Spandam" title="Spandam">Spandam</a>, though he is widely regarded amongst his CP9 colleagues despite his arrogance. 
</p><p>During his long undercover period, Lucci remained silent all the time, using <a href="/wiki/Hattori" title="Hattori">Hattori</a> as his preferred method of communication. In spite of his unfriendly looks, shipwright Lucci was polite, humble and tended to call out his fellow shipwrights for questionable conduct, particularly <a href="/wiki/Paulie" title="Paulie">Paulie</a>. Once his mission was completed, Lucci completely abandoned this persona, reverting back to the cold killer attitude that is natural to CP9's agents.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;"><b>Lucci</b>: The World Government decides justice for us. As long as the government recognizes you as the leader of CP9, we will carry out our orders to the letter... but we don't have to agree with your ideals.<br><b>Spandam</b>: You're right, but... What is it you want, then?!!<br><b>Lucci</b>: Blood. When we're here, murder is justified.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Lucci expresses his drive as a CP9 agent.<sup id="cite_ref-c382_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c382-22">[22]</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
Lucci bases his outlook of <a href="/wiki/Justice" title="Justice">justice</a> on his personal philosophy that any person or thing that goes against the World Government's interests should be destroyed, but is also evil for being that way. Specifically, he has declared to enforce <a href="/wiki/Justice#Absolute_Justice" title="Justice">Absolute Justice</a> in CP9’s form of "Dark Justice"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">闇の正義</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Yami no Seigi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> his motto being "Necessary Evil"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">必要悪</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Hitsuyō Aku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> As such, he is willing go to extreme lengths to fulfill his given mission by any means necessary, believing that CP9's authority to kill to be justified.<sup id="cite_ref-c382_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c382-22">[22]</a></sup> Lucci also finds it offensive when someone shows weakness around him<sup id="cite_ref-c422b_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422b-24">[24]</a></sup>, going as far as to dismiss a <a href="/wiki/Nero" title="Nero">new colleague</a> by presumably killing him for being weak.<sup id="cite_ref-c373_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c373-25">[25]</a></sup> The reason that he killed the five hundred soldiers in his past was due to another belief of his - the belief that weakness is a sin. Personally, he believes anyone who shows weakness is no better than a criminal.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>However, it appears that in spite of his stoic and professional appearance, Lucci is far from emotionless or beyond provocation. Beneath his expressionless demeanor, lies tremendous pride and arrogance along with extreme bloodthirst. In the Tower of Justice at Enies Lobby, he revealed that he only joined the World Government so he could be legally allowed to kill people; a sentiment which dates back to his childhood. An example of Lucci's lust for violence is when he compromised the mission of bringing <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Robin</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Gates_of_Justice" title="Gates of Justice">Gates of Justice</a>, by allowing Monkey D. Luffy to tail him for the sole purpose of having a battle, smirking when Luffy burst through the door.<sup id="cite_ref-c409_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c409-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>In and out of combat, Lucci is very sadistic and also seems to derive amusement and gratification from inflicting physical and emotional pain on others. These scenes, along with his anticipation of battle, are the only times where he feels genuinely happy.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> As an example of his sadism, Lucci once flooded an entire passageway in an attempt to kill the Straw Hat crew members moving through it, simply because he wanted to eliminate Luffy's chances of having everything, just to anger him.<sup id="cite_ref-c420_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c420-28">[28]</a></sup> Lucci has a habit of demoralizing and taunting his opponents, which is seen various times during his confrontation with Luffy, where he constantly brought up the possibility of killing Nico Robin.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">[29]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Lastly, while understated initially, it is very clear Lucci's title of the strongest in CP9's history has massively elevated his ego, leading to what appears to be a superiority complex. This pride also means he has a very low tolerance for insults. During his fight with Luffy, Lucci did not pay attention to Usopp until he started insulting him. In addition, he reacts rather violently to anyone calling him a <i>gaki</i> (slang in Japanese for "kid" or "brat"), responding with a kick and a retort both times after <a href="/wiki/Iceburg" title="Iceburg">Iceburg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> referred to him as such.<sup id="cite_ref-c346_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c346-30">[30]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> This is perhaps best exemplified by his reencounter with Luffy at Egghead, where Lucci was eager to fight him again while disregarding Kaku and Stussy's warnings that they needed permission from the World Government to do so due to Luffy's new <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">status</a>. Aside from Lucci's own personal vendetta towards Luffy for defeating him two years ago, Lucci cannot accept the fact that a "mere pirate" was able to defeat CP9's strongest and ignored all warnings and protocols just so he could battle Luffy one more time. Sometimes, Lucci's pride borders on unfitting childishness as, despite losing once more, he still stubbornly refused to acknowledge Luffy's power or his stature as an Emperor of the Sea despite the latter's victory against <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, although he would later relent and admit his enemy's status as an Emperor.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/78/CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png/revision/latest?cb=20230903235736" class="image"><img alt="CP9's Independent Report" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="233" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="CP9's Independent Report.png" data-image-key="CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/78/CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230903235736"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/78/CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png/revision/latest?cb=20230903235736" class="image"><img alt="CP9's Independent Report" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/78/CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230903235736" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="233" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="CP9's Independent Report.png" data-image-key="CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/78/CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230903235736"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:CP9%27s_Independent_Report.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci showing gratitude to the doctors who saved his life.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite all this apparent lack of morality, Lucci has displayed some, if very little, sympathy for those he dubs innocent. When the Candy Pirates were attacking a small village, he quickly dispatched the captain to save the people,<sup id="cite_ref-c513_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c513-32">[32]</a></sup> though his demonstration of <a href="/wiki/Justice#Absolute_Justice" title="Justice">Absolute Justice</a> later prompts him and his comrades to leave.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> This shows that deep down, he is not completely heartless and is more honorable to the people he respects. Likewise, he shows concern for his pet pigeon Hattori, sending him away when in dangerous situations. Lastly, he expressed gratitude to the doctor who saved his life after his clash with Luffy on Enies Lobby.<sup id="cite_ref-c506_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c506-19">[19]</a></sup>
</p><p>After the timeskip, Lucci's personality has largely stayed the same, as he condoned Saint Charlos' attempts to claim Shirahoshi as a slave during the Levely. He maintains that the Celestial Dragons are divine and have the right to obtain what they want from normal humans.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-34">[34]</a></sup> Still, he is one of the few government agents that is willing to question and delve into the ongoings of the institution, regardless of the dangers of doing so.
</p><p>Lucci also appears to be very honest when he is not under orders to maintain his cover. Even when his enemies had him in cuffs and his only hope of survival was to convince them to release him, he still answered all their questions truthfully without hesitation, even though his answers would have made them want to free him less.<sup id="cite_ref-c1076_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1076-35">[35]</a></sup> That said, this all turned out to be deception from his part, showing that Lucci can be patient and pragmatic in extremely unfavorable situations.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Organizations">Organizations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="CP9">CP9</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Blueno_Saves_CP9.png/revision/latest?cb=20230927040234" class="image"><img alt="Blueno Saves CP9" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="235" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Blueno Saves CP9.png" data-image-key="Blueno_Saves_CP9.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Blueno_Saves_CP9.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230927040234"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Blueno_Saves_CP9.png/revision/latest?cb=20230927040234" class="image"><img alt="Blueno Saves CP9" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Blueno_Saves_CP9.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230927040234" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="235" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Blueno Saves CP9.png" data-image-key="Blueno_Saves_CP9.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/81/Blueno_Saves_CP9.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230927040234"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Blueno_Saves_CP9.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci saved by Blueno.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With the exception of <a href="/wiki/Spandam" title="Spandam">Spandam</a>, Lucci has known his fellow CP9 colleagues since growing up together during childhood, though he rarely expressed any concern for them beyond his usual arrogance and superiority. Despite Lucci's cold reputation as a mass murderer, the core members of CP9 (excluding Spandam) genuinely care for Lucci's well-being, evidenced in their efforts to raise money to help pay for an operation that Lucci needed to save his life and their celebration when he was discharged from the hospital. He also had a fierce rivalry with <a href="/wiki/Jabra" title="Jabra">Jabra</a> that was most evidently expressed by their opposing Zoan fruit forms.<sup id="cite_ref-c379_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c379-11">[11]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Lucci did not care for CP9's newest agent, <a href="/wiki/Nero" title="Nero">Nero</a>, stating that his defeat was expected due to his inability to use the whole Rokushiki moveset. As such, Lucci decided to kill him after his defeat by Franky by stabbing Nero multiple times in the back with <i>Shigan</i> and throwing him into the ocean.<sup id="cite_ref-c373_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c373-25">[25]</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Kaku">Kaku</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Lucci has a generally good relationship with his fellow assassin Kaku, considering him his partner. They both spent 5 years under disguise as Galley-La employees and were among the most competent and reasonable of the shipwrights working there. Kaku respects Lucci's strength and often obeys and follows his orders, as if the latter was his superior. Lucci overall cares about Kaku's well-being and even requested <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Mars" title="Marcus Mars">Marcus Mars</a> to spare his friend, who was badly injury and trapped, at one point.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">[36]</a></sup>
</p><p>As members of CP0, their relationship more or less remains the same, with Kaku's more excitable personality generally contrasting with Lucci's aloofness. That said, Kaku is sometimes annoyed by Lucci's audacity in not following proper protocols and questioning the government. Kaku in particular was baffled at Lucci's outright honesty about declaring his intentions to kill all the Straw Hats, when they were both trying to convince Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> to release them from <a href="/wiki/Seastone" title="Seastone">seastone</a> handcuffs in the first place.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Jabra">Jabra</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png/revision/latest?cb=20230624125936" class="image"><img alt="Jabra and Lucci Rivalry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jabra and Lucci Rivalry.png" data-image-key="Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230624125936"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png/revision/latest?cb=20230624125936" class="image"><img alt="Jabra and Lucci Rivalry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230624125936" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jabra and Lucci Rivalry.png" data-image-key="Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230624125936"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jabra_and_Lucci_Rivalry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Shadowy silhouettes of Lucci and Jabra expressing their rivalry in their most feral form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci and Jabra appear to have a fierce rivalry, owning to their opposing Zoan themes of a feline and a canine respectively. During their first reunion at <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a> after 5 years, both agents quickly devolved into petty mockery and calling the other names, forcing the other CP9 members to talk some sense to them when hostilities became too intense. 
</p><p>Despite their rivalry, Jabra still seems to care about Lucci's well being, raising money to help pay for an operation that Lucci needed to save his life.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Spandam">Spandam</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png/revision/latest?cb=20240307044240" class="image"><img alt="Spandam and Lucci at Dressrosa" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Spandam and Lucci at Dressrosa.png" data-image-key="Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240307044240"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png/revision/latest?cb=20240307044240" class="image"><img alt="Spandam and Lucci at Dressrosa" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240307044240" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Spandam and Lucci at Dressrosa.png" data-image-key="Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/af/Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240307044240"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Spandam_and_Lucci_at_Dressrosa.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci working with Spandam.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Even though he highly disregards Spandam as a weakling, Lucci still acknowledged him as his boss without question.<sup id="cite_ref-c379_11-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c379-11">[11]</a></sup> However, he did appear to harbor some disdain for Spandam, having flippantly referred to his boss as "a certain idiot" and wishing he could witness Luffy's excellent initiative as a leader.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">[37]</a></sup> Spandam also believed in Lucci's strength, and he always referred to him as the strongest agent of Cipher Pol 9's history.<sup id="cite_ref-c422a_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422a-13">[13]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Their dynamic would change after the destruction of Enies Lobby, where Spandam and his father <a href="/wiki/Spandine" title="Spandine">Spandine</a> had Lucci and his fellow former subordinates framed as scapegoats to cover his own mishap. Likewise, Lucci vowed to Spandam and his father that they would return one day to find them.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup> After thwarting a treacherous operation orchestrated by Spandine,<sup id="cite_ref-sbs109_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs109-39">[39]</a></sup> Lucci was reinstated to the World Government alongside Spandam as members of CP0 with their roles reversed, with the latter now having to serve his former henchman as his superior.<sup id="cite_ref-c801_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c801-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120134542" class="image"><img alt="CP9 Stands on the Tower of Justice" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="CP9 Stands on the Tower of Justice.png" data-image-key="CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230120134542"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png/revision/latest?cb=20230120134542" class="image"><img alt="CP9 Stands on the Tower of Justice" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230120134542" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="CP9 Stands on the Tower of Justice.png" data-image-key="CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230120134542"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:CP9_Stands_on_the_Tower_of_Justice.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci ready to fight alongside the rest of CP9 in the World Government's turf.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the strongest Cipher Pol agent in CP9, the World Government saw Lucci as a very important asset to their cause and his strength is acknowledged by the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> and even the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlords</a>. Lucci was willing to do whatever it takes for their sake and followed the doctrine of Absolute Justice; he believed that the 500 soldiers who surrendered to pirates were no different than criminals who deserved death, and the Government apparently did not argue with his unauthorized killing of them. However, after Spandam framed CP9 for his debacles, Lucci and his colleagues briefly became fugitives of the World Government.
</p><p>As of the time skip, however, this seems to have been rectified after the former agents successfully stopped a plot lead by Spandine from committing an unsanctioned <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/act_of_aggression" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:act of aggression">act of aggression</a> alongside former Level 6 prisoners of <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> and certain parties of the <a href="/wiki/Underworld" title="Underworld">Underworld</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-sbs109_39-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sbs109-39">[39]</a></sup> For his service, Lucci has been reinstated and promoted to CP0, and Spandam has since been demoted from his former position as CP0 Chief into his current subordinate role.<sup id="cite_ref-c801_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c801-3">[3]</a></sup> While Lucci is loyal to the World Government, he also calls to question with some of their decision-making; namely their order to eliminate the world-famous scientist <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Arc" title="Egghead Arc">Egghead Arc</a>, Lucci's constant desire to fight Luffy for revenge after the Enies Lobby incident caused him to ignore the usual protocols from the World Government that prohibited fights with the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>, showing that while Lucci will loyally carry out any given mission, he either does not care or is not afraid to disregard certain rules of conduct to do so.
</p><p>Ultimately, despite Lucci's loyalty and status, <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> deemed him expendable regarding the situation at Egghead, prioritizing the safety of York, <a href="/wiki/Punk_Records" title="Punk Records">Punk Records</a>, and the power plant needed to produce the <a href="/wiki/Mother_Flame" title="Mother Flame">Mother Flame</a>, over one of their best agents. <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Mars" title="Marcus Mars">Marcus Mars</a> of the Elders also brushed off Lucci's request to spare Kaku as difficult.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite working for the World Government, Lucci is indifferent towards the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> and shows no hesitation to sacrifice their men to reach his goals. That being said, many marines like Vice-Admiral <a href="/wiki/Onigumo" title="Onigumo">Onigumo</a> and Admiral <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Borsalino</a> hold Lucci's strength and competency in high esteem, considering him a valuable asset.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Nobles">World Nobles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As an agent of CP0, Lucci has absolute loyalty to the World Nobles, regardless of their immense tyranny, believing that their status as gods privileges them to do whatever they want, even if it means enslaving a princess or assassinating a king. Thus, while Lucci dutifully obeyed Charlos' orders to enslave Shirahoshi and also to execute Neptune for his defiance, he did not interfere when Mjosgard, another World Noble, punished Charlos for his atrocity. In <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Film:_Gold" title="One Piece Film: Gold">One Piece Film: Gold</a>,</i> however, the completion of a mission is more important to him than the well-being of the Celestial Dragons, as he completely disregarded the safety of <a href="/wiki/Camael" title="Camael">Camael</a> and his noble companion and was more than willing to lose them to collateral damage if it meant accomplishing his goal.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Among the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, there are two particular people that Lucci once targeted for mission purposes: <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> and <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>, the first for her knowledge of the <a href="/wiki/Poneglyphs" class="mw-redirect" title="Poneglyphs">Poneglyphs</a> and the latter for being suspected of having the blueprints of <a href="/wiki/Pluton" title="Pluton">Pluton</a>. While Robin was already a long-time target of the organization, Franky only caught Lucci's eye after he figured out the shipwright's true identity as Cutty Flam.
</p><p>While disguised as an employee of Galley-La, Lucci was professional and helpful towards the Straw Hats, explaining to them about the issues of repairing the <a href="/wiki/Going_Merry" title="Going Merry">Going Merry</a>. After revealing himself as a government agent, however, Lucci became hostile towards the group. That said, he honored the deal he made with Robin beforehand to spare the Straw Hat crew and leave them alone as long as she renounced membership and cooperated with their mission. This deal fell through when the Straw Hats insisted in pursuing Lucci and CP9 to <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a>, at which point he considered them valid targets for killing.
</p><p>The members of the Straw Hat Pirates are all aware of how powerful and dangerous Lucci is. They acknowledged that if Luffy did not hold him off at Enies Lobby, many of them would have been killed by the assassin. Even after two years and having grown much stronger, the Weakling Trio remain terrified of Lucci and wanted to avoid being on the same island as him, despite not being his current target.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png/revision/latest?cb=20230117074341" class="image"><img alt="Lucci Fighting Luffy With Shigan Madara" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lucci Fighting Luffy With Shigan Madara.png" data-image-key="Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230117074341"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png/revision/latest?cb=20230117074341" class="image"><img alt="Lucci Fighting Luffy With Shigan Madara" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230117074341" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lucci Fighting Luffy With Shigan Madara.png" data-image-key="Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/cd/Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230117074341"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lucci_Fighting_Luffy_With_Shigan_Madara.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci and Luffy locked in combat.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci personally made an enemy out of the Straw Hats' <a href="/wiki/Pirate_Captain" title="Pirate Captain">captain</a>, Luffy. The two engaged in a vicious battle at the tower of Enies Lobby. Lucci was an extremely formidable opponent and made Luffy exert himself through raw physical power more than ever before, to the point where Luffy was unable to move after the battle. Despite being enemies, Lucci ultimately respected Luffy's strength and determination, saying that it would have been boring for him to have died in the Buster Call bombardment, and also added that Luffy is a worthy captain for having absolute faith in his crew and their ability to survive.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png/revision/latest?cb=20240907140411" class="image"><img alt="Awakened Zoans Retaining Personality" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="234" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Awakened Zoans Retaining Personality.png" data-image-key="Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240907140411"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png/revision/latest?cb=20240907140411" class="image"><img alt="Awakened Zoans Retaining Personality" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240907140411" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="234" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Awakened Zoans Retaining Personality.png" data-image-key="Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/33/Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240907140411"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Awakened_Zoans_Retaining_Personality.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci and Luffy face off again on Egghead in their awakened states.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci would later re-encounter Luffy during the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Arc" title="Egghead Arc">Egghead Arc</a> as <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a>'s attack against Dr. <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> began.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[40]</a></sup> In spite of being fully aware of Luffy's status as one of the Four Emperors, Lucci chose to disregard the World Government's protocol, which prevented confronting an Emperor without clearance, due to the events of Enies Lobby two years ago. The agent then revealed his new awakened form, teasing Luffy about being not the only one to have gotten stronger and immediately clashed with Straw Hat in his awakened state as well, continuing to ignore any protocols for the chance to avenge his prior defeat. Despite being ordered not to attack the Straw Hat Pirates on Egghead until the Marines arrived, Lucci continued to not listen, admitting he did not acknowledge Luffy as an Emperor.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[41]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Later on, when the <a href="/wiki/Seraphim" title="Seraphim">Seraphim</a> were ordered to kill both the captive CP0 and the Straw Hats, Lucci and Kaku had no choice but to ask to be freed and then team up with Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> to survive,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[42]</a></sup> with Lucci rather boldly admitting he would never attack the other members of the Straw Hat Pirates or the <a href="/wiki/SSG" title="SSG">SSG</a> before he eliminated Luffy first.<sup id="cite_ref-c1076_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1076-35">[35]</a></sup> Still, Lucci would later go back on his word and attempt to assassinate Dr. Vegapunk once more.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">[43]</a></sup> When he starts fighting Zoro, he calls him the No. 2 of an Emperor, indicating that he has now come to acknowledge Luffy's title.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">[44]</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy always refers to Lucci as "Pigeon Guy"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ハトの奴</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Hato no Yatsu</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, even after the timeskip. This mostly stems from Luffy being quite impressed by Lucci's ventriloquist act back when the latter was under disguise.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Nico_Robin">Nico Robin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Lucci, along with the whole of CP9, was a major enemy of <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>. However, Lucci was especially interested in arresting her because of her symbolic existence and threat against the World Government.
</p><p>As part of a deal he made with Robin, Lucci and the rest of CP9 would leave the Straw Hats alone if she simply left the crew and cooperated with their mission to find the blueprints for Pluton. However, since Robin did not expect the Straw Hats to go to such extremes for her at Enies Lobby, the deal was called off. While fighting Luffy, Lucci would frequently taunt him about Robin and how he would never allow her to live.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>, Lucci, now part of CP0, requested his fellow agents to capture Nico Robin, which ended unsuccessfully.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Franky">Franky</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Because of his relation to <a href="/wiki/Tom" title="Tom">Tom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iceburg" title="Iceburg">Iceburg</a> and the possibility of being the Pluton blueprint holder, Franky was a person of interest to Lucci. After dealing with Iceburg, Lucci attacked the <a href="/wiki/Franky_Family" title="Franky Family">Franky Family</a>, interrogated <a href="/wiki/Zambai" title="Zambai">Zambai</a> and invaded Franky's secret warehouse (the former <a href="/wiki/Tom%27s_Workers" title="Tom's Workers">Tom's Workers</a> HQ) to search for the blueprints, all of which earned Franky's ire.<sup id="cite_ref-c399_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c399-45">[45]</a></sup> Lucci also had Franky arrested for the accident he caused years ago (that <a href="/wiki/Tom" title="Tom">Tom</a> took responsibility for) as an excuse to bring him to Enies Lobby as well and question him further.
</p><p>Later, at Enies Lobby, Franky revealed he indeed had the blueprints all along and burned them in front of CP9, much to Lucci's shock, as the action rendered his mission to retrieve them all for naught. Franky, alongside Luffy, also confronted Lucci briefly, who commended on the cyborg's abilities, but turned out to be way below the assassin's league in terms of power.
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Roronoa_Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Lucci briefly clashed with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> when he first revealed his CP9 identity, blocking his strike and throwing him away along with Luffy. 
</p><p>Two years later, upon Marine <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru's</a> arrival to Egghead island, Lucci would shed his façade of an alliance with <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> (something that Zoro himself was against from the beginning). After incapacitating Stussy during a failed attempt on Vegapunk's life, Lucci engaged Zoro in combat, during which they fought at their maximum strength while Kizaru fought Luffy, with Lucci stating that killing Zoro would be as satisfying as killing Luffy, a feat Zoro claimed would be impossible for Lucci to achieve. During their battle Zoro struck Lucci with a heavy blow leaving him weakened, but before Lucci could attempt anything else Zoro was forced to escape, ending their fight.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Iceburg">Iceburg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><a href="/wiki/Iceburg" title="Iceburg">Iceburg</a> was the holder of the plans to Pluton for four years after Tom's death. After those four years, he secretly gave them to the man who he thought to be dead, Cutty Flam. As this was done in secret, the government still believed that Iceburg was in possession of the plans. As such, he was forever pestered by officials who came to try and convince him to hand over the plans. After years of being stalked by government officers for the Pluton plans, the strongest divisions of the Cipher Pol were secretly sent for Iceburg.
</p><p>Without him knowing, four of the CP9 agents infiltrated Water 7 and disguised themselves to look like normal people, with several even gaining entries into his trusted inner circle. Three more masked people entered the room and revealed themselves to be not only CP9, but also people that Iceburg trusted: Lucci, Kalifa, Kaku, and bartender Blueno. Lucci revealed his theory about the real Pluton blueprints' whereabouts, while Kaku felt his pulse, and Iceburg's heightened and nervous reactions only confirmed it. Lucci later offered to step on Iceburg's face to prove his antagonism, showing no attachment for his former boss.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Paulie">Paulie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>During his five years working undercover as a shipwright under Iceburg, Lucci acted as a friend to fellow shipwright <a href="/wiki/Paulie" title="Paulie">Paulie</a>. Despite Lucci's actions against Paulie's gambling addiction, the two were seemingly very close. However, upon CP9 finally making their move and revealing themselves, in which Paulie initially attempted to claim to be some misunderstanding, Lucci showed his complete aloofness in revealing that their five years friendship was an act, and brutally attacked Paulie while rebuffing his claim that he still thought they were friends.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Candy_Pirates">Candy Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The crew invaded St. Poplar during one of their raids. Lucci attacked the captain while the other CP9 agents struck out at his crew. However, the citizens became horrified when Lucci took the attack too far, and began to show "excessive justice" against their captain by stepping on the pirate's skull.<sup id="cite_ref-c513_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c513-32">[32]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Stussy">Stussy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png/revision/latest?cb=20240512150510" class="image"><img alt="Stussy Dodges Lucci" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="194" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Stussy Dodges Lucci.png" data-image-key="Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512150510"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png/revision/latest?cb=20240512150510" class="image"><img alt="Stussy Dodges Lucci" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512150510" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="194" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Stussy Dodges Lucci.png" data-image-key="Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/64/Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240512150510"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Stussy_Dodges_Lucci.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci tries to kill Stussy, but fails.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Stussy" title="Stussy">Stussy</a> is one of Lucci's former fellow CP0 agents. They generally held a professional relationship, although Stussy cautioned Lucci several times about questioning and disobeying the World Government.
</p><p>However, Lucci was shocked to find out Stussy was double agent for <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a> all along, betraying him and Kaku, which led to Lucci unsuccessfully attempting to kill her on the spot.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">[46]</a></sup> In the end, Lucci claimed he would never forgive Stussy for her betrayal and made good on his words after stabbing her later on with a Shigan, albeit unintended. After he and Kaku returned to their ship following the end of their mission, Lucci told a fellow Cipher Pol agent he killed Stussy.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_2">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hattori">Hattori</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Having known each other for twenty years, <a href="/wiki/Hattori" title="Hattori">Hattori</a> is the closest relationship Lucci has despite his infamous reputation as a mass-murderer. The pigeon is shown to be both loyal and unafraid of Lucci as he stays alongside his master even in dangerous situations. When Lucci is not fighting, Hattori is usually perched on his master's right shoulder. Lucci would have had to express some emotions to blend in with citizens while undercover, but Hattori did this for him as his ventriloquist dummy; this allowed Lucci to be somewhat sociable while remaining emotionless.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">[48]</a></sup> While Hattori reverted to being an ordinary pigeon after Lucci was revealed to be an assassin, he occasionally exhibits human traits such as drinking from a cup.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">

  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">In battle, nothing is ever certain. Before the incident at Enies Lobby, no one thought that Rob Lucci could lose.

  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>

  </td>
