<p><br>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png/revision/latest?cb=20220718044409" class="image"><img alt="Rob Lucci Slaughters Soldiers" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rob Lucci Slaughters Soldiers.png" data-image-key="Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220718044409"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png/revision/latest?cb=20220718044409" class="image"><img alt="Rob Lucci Slaughters Soldiers" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220718044409" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rob Lucci Slaughters Soldiers.png" data-image-key="Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/fe/Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220718044409"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rob_Lucci_Slaughters_Soldiers.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Even at a young age, Lucci was extremely deadly.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the strongest member in <a href="/wiki/CP9" title="CP9">CP9</a>'s entire history, Lucci garnered an infamous reputation even acknowledged by <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a>, who noted that no one could have foreseen Lucci's defeat.<sup id="cite_ref-c474_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c474-49">[49]</a></sup> Even at the tender age of 13, Lucci was already known to be a very capable mass murderer, having killed 500 of a kingdom's soldiers as well as a pirate crew single-handedly. By adulthood, Lucci had become by far the strongest agent in CP9 history,<sup id="cite_ref-c422a_13-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422a-13">[13]</a></sup> with his <a href="/wiki/Doriki" title="Doriki">Doriki</a> at 4000 (almost twice that of the second strongest agent, <a href="/wiki/Kaku" title="Kaku">Kaku</a>'s 2200).<sup id="cite_ref-c379_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c379-11">[11]</a></sup> Franky remarked that Lucci's strength was levels above the rest of CP9 and that, had it not been for Luffy holding him off with their fight, he was unsure how many of their comrades would have been slaughtered.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[50]</a></sup> Since his first known loss to Luffy, Lucci grew more powerful and is now officially part of <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a>, which is considered to be the strongest and most exclusive of the <a href="/wiki/Cipher_Pol" title="Cipher Pol">Cipher Pols</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c801_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c801-3">[3]</a></sup> He would also assume a position of authority within CP0, usually giving orders and instruction to other masked agents. However, he proved to be no match for Luffy after the young pirate become one of the <a href="/wiki/Four_Emperors" title="Four Emperors">Four Emperors</a>. While he was able to fight against <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, the "No. 2" of the Straw Hat Pirates, on even grounds, he was not able to defeat the pirate hunter and suffered serious wounds from him, effectively losing the fight.
</p><p>Because of his reputation, Lucci is a very valuable asset to the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, almost to the point of legend.<sup id="cite_ref-c422a_13-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422a-13">[13]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Onigumo" title="Onigumo">Onigumo</a> even believed that he could survive a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a> attack.<sup id="cite_ref-c422b_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422b-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p><p>Lucci is also a skilled <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ventriloquism" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ventriloquism">ventriloquist</a>, meaning he is capable of making his voice sound like it is coming from somewhere else, most notably from his pet pigeon <a href="/wiki/Hattori" title="Hattori">Hattori</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Having undergone extremely hard Rokushiki training from early childhood, Lucci has developed extraordinary physical prowess, well beyond any other CP9 agent; specifically, 400 times stronger than a common, armed soldier (eight times greater than the necessary minimum to be considered "superhuman") according to his <a href="/wiki/Doriki" title="Doriki">Doriki</a>, without transforming.<sup id="cite_ref-c379_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c379-11">[11]</a></sup>
</p><p>Lucci possesses tremendous durability and reserves of stamina. Even after taking a considerable amount of damage from Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Gear 2</a> attacks, Lucci barely flinched and resumed the battle after being slammed into two buildings by Luffy's <b><a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques#Pre-Timeskip" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques">Gigant Pistol</a></b>, though he was almost knocked out and took heavy damage later. At only the age of 13, he came out untroubled, without showing any signs of pain after being shot at from behind by multiple cannon shots, only receiving the scars on his back.<sup id="cite_ref-c422b_24-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422b-24">[24]</a></sup> Strength-wise, he could temporarily knock out Franky, a powerful <a href="/wiki/Cyborgs" title="Cyborgs">cyborg</a> immune to bullets, with a single blow before sending him crashing through a wall with a kick. He could block Sanji's kick with his forearm without using <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Tekkai" title="Rokushiki/Tekkai">Tekkai</a>. As a user of <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Shigan" title="Rokushiki/Shigan">Shigan</a>, his fingers are extremely strong, allowing him to penetrate stone pavement with a simple grip. Lucci also easily caught Luffy's face with one arm, despite his own great strength, while at the same time shrugging off all his punches, and then casually threw him into a wall.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[51]</a></sup> During a brief confrontation against those who were trying to defend Shirahoshi from Charlos, Lucci was able to catch <a href="/wiki/Leo" title="Leo">Leo</a>, who is a very fast, small <a href="/wiki/Dwarves" title="Dwarves">dwarf</a>, and effortlessly push <a href="/wiki/Sai" title="Sai">Sai</a>, the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Happo_Navy" title="Happo Navy">Happo Navy</a>, with a single kick.<sup id="cite_ref-c907_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c907-34">[34]</a></sup>
</p><p>Lucci is a highly skilled and formidable hand-to-hand combatant, as shown when he fought Luffy in their second match, before Luffy used Gear 2. Lucci fought an even battle with him without using his Devil Fruit powers, and was even slightly superior, as he got more hits on his opponent than the Straw Hat captain did to him. Furthermore, he barely used the more offensive techniques like Shigan and <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Rankyaku" title="Rokushiki/Rankyaku">Rankyaku</a> until Luffy started using his Gears.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Along with his great superhuman prowess, Lucci is a highly intelligent and cunning individual, being able to become a master carpenter within a 5-year period merely as a form of espionage and surveillance over his "boss" Iceburg (whom CP9 believed to have possession of the blueprints for the Ancient Weapon Pluton), and even when it was discovered otherwise, Lucci quickly deduced the next most likely candidate (Franky) based solely on their adolescent friendship. He and the other CP9 agents that infiltrated Water 7 deceived every single inhabitant, a clear sign of their manipulative skills.
</p><p>A master tactician, Lucci managed to almost single-handedly eliminate the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> (excluding Luffy, whom he was battling) by understanding the structure of his environment and firing a well-aimed "Rankyaku" through a stone wall, flooding the ground floor of the Tower of Justice and all its hidden underground passages with seawater.<sup id="cite_ref-c420_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c420-28">[28]</a></sup> Had it not been for the unexpected arrival of Kokoro and her mermaid heritage, they would not have survived. He also quickly analyzed the mechanics behind Luffy's Gear 2 technique after engaging it for just a couple of minutes at most, explaining it to the rubber-man and stating that such bodily pressure would shave years off his lifespan.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[52]</a></sup> The fact that he was able to reach the same level as the Galley La carpenters (who spend their whole life building their skills) in five years just to do an undercover job shows a great talent for it.
</p><p>As an experienced spy, Lucci is very effective at gathering information and sending it to his superiors without arousing suspicion. <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> and Saint <a href="/wiki/Marcus_Mars" title="Marcus Mars">Marcus Mars</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> have both praised Lucci for his intel gathering capabilities during the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Incident" title="Egghead Incident">Egghead Incident</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Carpentry">Carpentry</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Since Lucci worked as a shipwright during his mission on Water 7, this means that he has some carpentry skills and knowledge about <a href="/wiki/Ship" title="Ship">ships</a>. He worked as a sawyer, treenail, and bolt specialist. He, along with Kaku, was able to recognize that the Pluton blueprints Franky revealed on Enies Lobby were indeed real.<sup id="cite_ref-c399_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c399-45">[45]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rokushiki">Rokushiki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki" title="Rokushiki">Rokushiki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shigan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230423172940" class="image"><img alt="Shigan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="132" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shigan.png" data-image-key="Shigan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shigan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230423172940"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shigan.png/revision/latest?cb=20230423172940" class="image"><img alt="Shigan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shigan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230423172940" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="132" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shigan.png" data-image-key="Shigan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Shigan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230423172940"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shigan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci effortlessly dispatches <a href="/wiki/Paulie" title="Paulie">Paulie</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci has the greatest mastery of Rokushiki within CP9's entire history, having developed more powerful variations from each of the different forms. He was able to skillfully use Soru and Shigan against 500 soldiers as a child, he fatally pierced their armor along with their bodies; he also used <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Tekkai" title="Rokushiki/Tekkai">Tekkai</a> to break two swords effortlessly. 
</p><p>By adulthood, Lucci's extraordinary skill in Rokushiki, combined with his Devil Fruit powers, allowed him to use improved variations of the martial art, such as <b><a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Rankyaku#Variations" title="Rokushiki/Rankyaku">Rankyaku: Gaicho</a></b>, which could cleave through the iron hull of a <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ships" title="Marine Ships">Marine battleship</a>, and <b><a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Shigan#Variations" title="Rokushiki/Shigan">Tobu Shigan: Bachi</a></b>, which could pierce Luffy's rubber body with mere flicks of compressed air. In his hybrid form, a simple Rankyaku was enough to slice through the <a href="/wiki/Galley-La_Headquarters" title="Galley-La Headquarters">Galley-La Headquarters</a> and cause most of the building to collapse. His high skill in Tekkai allowed him to casually block an attack from <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronora Zoro</a>, a swordsman that can easily slice steel. Indeed, Franky's <b>Strong Hammer</b>, which sent his fellow CP9 agent <a href="/wiki/Fukurou" title="Fukurou">Fukurou</a> flying through two walls, despite his use of Tekkai, failed to make Lucci budge an inch, as the assassin's <a href="/wiki/Doriki" title="Doriki">Doriki</a> was five times his. Most notably, he used a hidden, seventh Rokushiki technique, <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Rokuogan" title="Rokushiki/Rokuogan"><b>Rokuogan</b></a>, during his fight with Luffy. The massively powerful technique was so strong that it caused severe internal injury to Luffy's body, who described its effect as an <a href="/wiki/Dials#Impact_Dial" title="Dials">Impact Dial</a> with greatly amplified power, which is no small feat, considering that he is made of rubber. With his complete mastery of Rokushiki, in conjunction with his Devil Fruit ability, Lucci proved to be a tremendously resilient and formidable foe, fighting on equal footing with Luffy in Gear 2, even being slightly superior, forcing Luffy to use <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques">Gear 3</a> to weaken him and in the end use all his forces against him.
</p><p>Two years later, after his promotion to <a href="/wiki/CP0" title="CP0">CP0</a> and the awakening of his <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a>, Lucci's skill in Rokushiki has only grown, as not only are his old techniques more powerful than before, but he has also exhibited completely new moves.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Seimei_Kikan">Seimei Kikan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Seimei_Kikan" title="Seimei Kikan">Seimei Kikan</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>It has been revealed that Lucci can perform Seimei Kikan, like <a href="/wiki/Kumadori" title="Kumadori">Kumadori</a>, and use it to alter his Zoan transformation that amplify his skills in a specific Rokushiki ability. However, only the <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Kami-e" title="Rokushiki/Kami-e">Kami-e Form</a>, which makes his man-beast form smaller and thinner, more like an average man-size, has been seen.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Neko_Neko_no_Mi,_Model:_Leopard" title="Neko Neko no Mi, Model: Leopard">Neko Neko no Mi, Model: Leopard</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20220410054931" class="image"><img alt="Neko Neko no Mi, Model Leopard Human-Beast Form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neko Neko no Mi, Model Leopard Human-Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220410054931"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20220410054931" class="image"><img alt="Neko Neko no Mi, Model Leopard Human-Beast Form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220410054931" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="210" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neko Neko no Mi, Model Leopard Human-Beast Form.png" data-image-key="Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6e/Neko_Neko_no_Mi%2C_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220410054931"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neko_Neko_no_Mi,_Model_Leopard_Human-Beast_Form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci in his Human-Beast Leopard form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci ate the Neko Neko no Mi, Model: Leopard, a <a href="/wiki/Zoan" title="Zoan">Zoan</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> which allows him to transform into a full leopard, or a bulky leopard-human hybrid at will.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p><p>As Zoan class Devil Fruits enhance physical capabilities the most, it is most favored by martial artists like Lucci, who is able to integrate the unique traits of his Devil Fruit, such as claws and stronger legs, to greatly enhance the effects of his techniques. Also, being a carnivorous animal, Lucci is more bloodthirsty and predatory than a regular Zoan class user, proven when he mauled Luffy as an actual leopard.<sup id="cite_ref-c422b_24-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c422b-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p><p>By using Seimei Kikan, Lucci can transform his bulky hybrid body into a more slender form. This smaller body greatly increases his speed, but at the cost of decreasing his Zoan enhanced strength.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Awakening">Awakening</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20240502161649" class="image"><img alt="Neko Neko no Mi Model Leopard Awakened Form" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="185" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neko Neko no Mi Model Leopard Awakened Form.png" data-image-key="Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240502161649"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png/revision/latest?cb=20240502161649" class="image"><img alt="Neko Neko no Mi Model Leopard Awakened Form" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240502161649" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="185" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neko Neko no Mi Model Leopard Awakened Form.png" data-image-key="Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20240502161649"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neko_Neko_no_Mi_Model_Leopard_Awakened_Form.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci in his Awakened form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci has also achieved Devil Fruit <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit#Awakening" title="Devil Fruit">Awakening</a>, letting him assume a new, much more powerful hybrid form, which greatly enhances his physical strength, speed, as well as his recovery rate. Unlike most Awakened Zoans, Lucci's personality was not overtaken by the animal nature of the Devil Fruit.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup> In this awakened form, he could somewhat match Luffy, while in his own <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_5_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 5 Techniques">Awakened form</a> for a time,<sup id="cite_ref-c1069_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1069-56">[56]</a></sup> even meeting him in a fist clash and withstanding his <b>Gomu Gomu no Mogura Pistol</b>;<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[57]</a></sup> however, he was soon overpowered after Luffy started putting more force behind his attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">[58]</a></sup> Nevertheless, Lucci was able to confront Zoro, a pirate with a bounty of over a billion, for an extended period of time while in this form, even managing to remain standing after being hit with a seemingly finishing move.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article: <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Armament_Haki">Armament Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3a/Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20240421100548" class="image"><img alt="Lucci's Armament Haki" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lucci's Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3a/Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240421100548"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3a/Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest?cb=20240421100548" class="image"><img alt="Lucci's Armament Haki" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3a/Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240421100548" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="199" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lucci's Armament Haki.png" data-image-key="Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/3a/Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240421100548"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lucci%27s_Armament_Haki.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Lucci hardens his leg to block Zoro's swords.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lucci possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> He demonstrated incredible skill with this form of Haki during his rematch against <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> after the timeskip. While "Awakened", Lucci hardened his fists and clashed with the emperor who is a powerful Armament Haki master in his own right.<sup id="cite_ref-c1069_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1069-56">[56]</a></sup> His hardened claws could also bypass <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a>'s advanced-grade defensive Armament Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">[59]</a></sup> Even in his human form, he could block Zoro's Haki enhanced swords with his hardened leg.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">[60]</a></sup> 
</p><p>Non-canonically, he was also seen hardening his arm, while fighting <a href="/wiki/Sabo" title="Sabo">Sabo</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Film:_Gold" title="One Piece Film: Gold">One Piece Film: Gold</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">[61]</a></sup><br style="clear:both;">
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Observation_Haki">Observation Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Lucci possesses the ability to use <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> He demonstrated this ability on <a href="/wiki/Egghead" title="Egghead">Egghead</a>, when he sensed <a href="/wiki/Jaygarcia_Saturn" title="Jaygarcia Saturn">Jaygarcia Saturn</a>'s arrival.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">[62]</a></sup> Later on, he sensed the arrival of the rest of the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a>, showing curiosity about their powerful Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[63]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Backstory">Backstory</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">They were criminals, so I killed them in name of justice... As soldiers, weakness is a sin. They surrendered to evil, and caused a crisis in the kingdom. That type of soldier doesn't deserve to live. So they're dead.</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;">— Lucci's view on <a href="/wiki/Justice" title="Justice">justice</a> as explained in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Anime)" title="One Piece (Anime)">anime</a></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br>
The anime follows the same trend for Lucci's back story, but with several differences and elaborations.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 180px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Teenage_Lucci.png/revision/latest?cb=20230927040246" class="image"><img alt="Teenage Lucci" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="569" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Teenage Lucci.png" data-image-key="Teenage_Lucci.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Teenage_Lucci.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230927040246"></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Teenage_Lucci.png/revision/latest?cb=20230927040246" class="image"><img alt="Teenage Lucci" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Teenage_Lucci.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230927040246" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="180" height="569" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Teenage Lucci.png" data-image-key="Teenage_Lucci.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/74/Teenage_Lucci.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20230927040246"></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Teenage_Lucci.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Thirteen-year-old Lucci in the anime.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After being sent, he approached the king, who begged Lucci to save the soldiers, but Lucci told the king not to question the ways of the World Government. This left the king to wonder what the Government was thinking, sending a young boy to such a dangerous assignment. Lucci stepped into the pirates' ship and claimed to serve justice against them, and they laughed and mocked him. After sarcastically telling Lucci to go home, two pirates attempted to strike him down with swords, but Lucci blocked it with his <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki#Tekkai" title="Rokushiki">Tekkai</a>.
</p><p>The crew thought Lucci was using some <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">weird ability</a>, and the captain warned that if Lucci resisted anymore, the hostages would die. Then, with the crew pointing guns at Lucci's head, he ordered his men to take Lucci to the prison along with the other soldiers, as a way to insult the World Government. After the pirates locked Lucci in and mocked him further, Lucci ensured that all the hostages were there - then, using his <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki" title="Rokushiki">Rokushiki</a> techniques, he brutally massacred all 500 hostages while the oblivious pirate crew was still enjoying their celebration party.
</p><p>When one of the pirates came to check out on the prisoners, he ran screaming for his captain - and the entire crew saw, to their horror and fury, all of their precious hostages murdered, with Lucci standing on top of the mountain of corpses, his victims' blood dripping from his hand. After a short argument on the <a href="/wiki/Justice" title="Justice">justice</a> of the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>, the captain angrily ordered his crew to use their mortars - the very weapons that forced the soldiers to surrender - to kill Lucci, with five cannonballs striking Lucci right in the back. The captain said that Lucci deserved it for looking down on them, then complained how their perfect plan was ruined.
</p><p>In the midst of his complaint, he saw, to his shock and horror, that Lucci had survived the blast and had stood back up from the inferno, with his back scarred a shape reminiscent of the World Government's logo. Lucci then used his <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Soru" title="Rokushiki/Soru">Soru</a> to swiftly appear before the captain and seized him by the face, then, despite the captain's futile attempt to pry himself free, Lucci launched a barrage of <a href="/wiki/Rokushiki/Shigan" title="Rokushiki/Shigan">Shigan</a> (much like <i>Shigan Oren</i>) to brutally stab the captain to death, letting his corpse crash down onto the ground. The remnants of the crew realized that the child in front of them is in fact a heartless monster who is immune to weapons and hostage situations, they knew they had no chance of winning, and screamed in horror while fleeing. Whether they were pursued and killed is not known. With that, Lucci's mission came to completion.
</p><p>Regardless of which version, the scar that Lucci gained on his back vaguely resembles the symbol of the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. Also, Lucci's view of justice explained in the anime is also mentioned by Oda in an SBS, who says he cut it out of the manga in order for the story to move along faster.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Punk_Hazard_Arc">Punk Hazard Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the manga, Lucci appears in silhouette as one of the brokers watching <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar</a>'s broadcast,<sup id="cite_ref-c692_64-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c692-64">[64]</a></sup> which is confirmed in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Doors!" title="One Piece Doors!">One Piece Doors!</a> Vol. 2<sup id="cite_ref-dv2_65-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dv2-65">[65]</a></sup> as well as <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card_-_One_Piece_Visual_Dictionary" title="Vivre Card - One Piece Visual Dictionary">Vivre Card databook</a> listing an appearance for Lucci in the <a href="/wiki/Punk_Hazard_Arc" title="Punk Hazard Arc">Punk Hazard Arc</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup> However, due to the ambiguity of the panel, the anime replaces Lucci with a different character with a thick mustache and a different voice actor.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[66]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 232px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 232px; height: 232px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Lucci_Silhouette_Punk_Hazard.png/revision/latest?cb=20240907140935" class="image"><img alt="Lucci Silhouette Punk Hazard" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="129" height="210" data-image-name="Lucci Silhouette Punk Hazard.png" data-image-key="Lucci_Silhouette_Punk_Hazard.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c1/Lucci_Silhouette_Punk_Hazard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/129?cb=20240907140935" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Lucci's silhouette in <a href="/wiki/Chapter_692" title="Chapter 692">Chapter 692</a>.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_Concepts">Early Concepts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>An early design of Lucci had him without his goatee and distinctive lips.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">[67]</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 232px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 232px; height: 232px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Early_W7_designs.png/revision/latest?cb=20230513185028" class="image"><img alt="Early W7 designs" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="179" height="210" data-image-name="Early W7 designs.png" data-image-key="Early_W7_designs.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Early_W7_designs.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/179?cb=20230513185028" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Early concept designs of Lucci and other Galley-La Company employees.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 232px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 232px; height: 232px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/CP9_Early.png/revision/latest?cb=20230130170056" class="image"><img alt="CP9 Early" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="188" height="210" data-image-name="CP9 Early.png" data-image-key="CP9_Early.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ee/CP9_Early.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/188?cb=20230130170056" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Early concept designs of Lucci and other CP9 agents.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>He was featured in the second wave of the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_VS_Figure_Gashapon" class="mw-redirect" title="One Piece VS Figure Gashapon">One Piece VS Figure Gashapon</a> series, in the <a href="/wiki/Portrait_of_Pirates" title="Portrait of Pirates">Portrait of Pirates</a>: Neo-6 wave of figurines, in the Dokodemo Swing and Animal Mascot strap sets, in Bandai's FC candy toy sets, and in the Plex Anime Heroes Enies Lobby set. He will also be represented in the upcoming Deforme Figure Keyholder set and the High Spec Coloring 5 set.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Lucci fought Luffy, Nami, and Usopp in the 2019 <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Water_Battle" title="One Piece Water Battle">One Piece Water Battle</a> show.</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2014" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2014</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bildy" title="Bildy">Bildy</a> made a <a href="/wiki/Kone_Kone_no_Mi" title="Kone Kone no Mi">fake version</a> of Lucci to fight as a general in the <a href="/wiki/DX_Marines" title="DX Marines">DX Marines</a>. In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2016" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pokke" title="Pokke">Pokke</a> made a <a href="/wiki/Mono_Mono_no_Mi" title="Mono Mono no Mi">clone</a> of Lucci and Hattori to fight the Straw Hat Pirates.</li>
<li>An image of Lucci appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Water_Spectacle" title="One Piece Water Spectacle">One Piece Water Spectacle</a>.</li>
<li>Lucci appears in the Zoro version of the <a href="/wiki/Hungry_Days" title="Hungry Days">Hungry Days</a> commercials.</li></ul>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Lucci_and_Hattori_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20201222211302" class="image"><img alt="Lucci and Hattori Water Battle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="55" height="120" data-image-name="Lucci and Hattori Water Battle.png" data-image-key="Lucci_and_Hattori_Water_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6a/Lucci_and_Hattori_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/55?cb=20201222211302" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Lucci and Hattori in Water Battle 2019.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 142px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 142px; height: 142px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8c/Lucci_Leopard_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20201222211320" class="image"><img alt="Lucci Leopard Water Battle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="63" height="120" data-image-name="Lucci Leopard Water Battle.png" data-image-key="Lucci_Leopard_Water_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/8c/Lucci_Leopard_Water_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/63?cb=20201222211320" class="lazyload"></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Lucci's leopard form in Water Battle 2019.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>In the 3rd, 4th, 5th, 6th, and 7th <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">fan polls</a> of most popular characters, Lucci was ranked 12th, 19th, 41st, 43rd, and 43rd, respectively. Making him the second most popular of the <a href="/wiki/CP9" title="CP9">CP9</a> members in the 3rd and 4th (after <a href="/wiki/Kaku" title="Kaku">Kaku</a> in both cases), the most popular in the 5th, 6th, and 7th.</li>
<li>According to the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Complete_Collection" title="One Piece Complete Collection">22nd Log</a>, Lucci's role as an antagonist during the <a href="/wiki/Water_7_Saga" title="Water 7 Saga">Water 7 Saga</a> was a relatively late decision by Oda and not part of his original plans. Apparently, Lucci was going to be just one of the many <a href="/wiki/Shipwright" title="Shipwright">shipwrights</a> introduced during the <a href="/wiki/Water_7_Arc" title="Water 7 Arc">Water 7 Arc</a> before Oda changed him into an undercover <a href="/wiki/CP9" title="CP9">CP9</a> agent.</li>
<li>Lucci's favorite food is brandy, and his least favorite food is spam.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_6-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lucci is the only known active Cipher Pol agent with a surname, in constrast to the now retired <a href="/wiki/Tsumonsieur_Kamaya" title="Tsumonsieur Kamaya">Tsumonsieur Kamaya</a>.</li>
<li>Lucci's flower resemblance is <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rudbeckia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rudbeckia">Rudbeckia</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-vc3_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc3-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li>If Lucci was not an intelligence agent, then he would be a pigeon breeder.<sup id="cite_ref-vc3_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc3-5">[5]</a></sup></li>
<li>Lucci enjoys winter on <a href="/wiki/Island_Climatic_Types" title="Island Climatic Types">Winter Islands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-vc3_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vc3-5">[5]</a></sup></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="SBS-Based_Trivia">SBS-Based Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FRob_Lucci%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>Lucci's birthday, June 2, comes from his surname since 6-2 can be derived from ro-bu.<sup id="cite_ref-birth_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birth-10">[10]</a></sup></li>
<li>A fan noted that <i>Rob</i> is another word for "steal" and <i>Lucci</i> sounds similar to <i>luce</i>, meaning "light" in Italian, thus potentially giving his name the meaning of "steal the light", which follows his theme of dark justice. However, when the fan asked if Oda named him this on purpose, Oda answered did not know about it.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[68]</a></sup></li></ul>
